Preceptor Surendra, a Maharashtrian, revered by all as MƒÅdhura, resorted to asceticism, an adept in Yogic practices, governed the Ma·π≠ha for only ten years and reached his abode on the first day of the bright fortnight in the month of MƒÅrga≈õƒ´r·π£a of the TƒÅra·πáa year in the Kali era 3486.

‡§ó‡•ã‡§µ‡§ø‡§®‡•ç‡§¶-‡§™‡§®‡•ç‡§§-‡§π‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ #‡•®‡•¨‡•ß

Observed on day 20 of December (gregorian) month. The event has been commemorated since it occurred in 1760 (gregorian era).
On this day, in the lead up to Panipat, the Marathas suffer a major setback as their veteran revenue collector Govind Pant, who was in charge of an extremely critical & strategic role, is killed in an overwhelming attack led by Atai Khan, the Durrani Wazir’s nephew.

Son of Ka·πá·πá≈´≈õa·πÖkara, the clever PadmanƒÅbha by ame, though intent on practising Lambika Yoga, this preceptor CidƒÅnandaghanendra adhering to the injunctions of the Master, remained in the seat of KƒÅmako·π≠i that bestows all desired things to those who resort to, fed innumerable devotees every day. This preceptor reached his Ultimate abode which is devoid of all grief, delusion etc. on the sixty day of bright fortnight in the month of MƒÅrga≈õƒ´r·π£a of the year Prajotpati.
